## Instruction

Please help me monitor new paid orders in WooCommerce, retrieve the SKU and quantity of each finished product in the order, then, based on the Bill of Materials (BOM) recorded in Google Sheets, calculate the amount of raw materials that need to be consumed. Deduct the corresponding quantities from the raw material inventory table in Google Sheets, write the updated raw material inventory back to Google Sheets, and then, based on the updated raw material balances, recalculate the maximum producible quantities for all finished products. Finally, sync these maximum producible quantities to WooCommerce as the available stock for the products.

</div>

### Google Sheet and WooCommerce

You can review the data construction process during testing [here](https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/tree/finalpool_dev/tasks/finalpool/update-material-inventory/preprocess).

```python
import json, math, os, sys

# Paths saved by prior tool calls
bom_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/779nwUaGnJyhSGWbZtbA2C.json"
inv_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/m6g7JoAtSpqdF4MQVoC4nm.json"

# Load JSON
with open(bom_path, 'r') as f:
    bom_json = json.load(f)
with open(inv_path, 'r') as f:
    inv_json = json.load(f)

# Helper to extract cell effective value

def get_cell_value(cell):
    if not cell:
        return None
    ev = cell.get('effectiveValue') or cell.get('userEnteredValue')
    if not ev:
        return None
    if 'stringValue' in ev:
        return ev['stringValue'].strip()
    if 'numberValue' in ev:
        return ev['numberValue']
    if 'boolValue' in ev:
        return ev['boolValue']
    return None

# Parse BOM: columns expected
# 0: Product SKU, 1: Product Name, 2: Raw Material ID, 3: Raw Material Name, 4: Unit Quantity, 5: Unit
bom_sheet = None
for s in bom_json['sheets']:
    if s['properties']['title'] == 'BOM':
        bom_sheet = s
        break
if not bom_sheet:
    print(json.dumps({"error":"BOM sheet not found"}))
    sys.exit(0)

bom_rows = bom_sheet['data'][0]['rowData']

from collections import defaultdict
bom_map = defaultdict(list)  # sku -> list of dicts {material_id, qty_per, unit}

# Iterate rows skipping header
for i, row in enumerate(bom_rows[1:], start=2):
    vals = row.get('values', [])
    # Ensure length >= 5
    if len(vals) < 5:
        continue
    sku = get_cell_value(vals[0])
    material_id = get_cell_value(vals[2])
    qty_per = get_cell_value(vals[4])
    unit = get_cell_value(vals[5]) if len(vals) > 5 else None
    if not sku or not material_id or qty_per is None:
        continue
    try:
        qty_per_num = float(qty_per)
    except Exception:
        continue
    if qty_per_num < 0:
        continue
    bom_map[sku].append({"material_id": material_id, "qty_per": qty_per_num, "unit": unit})

# Parse Material_Inventory: columns
# 0: Material ID, 1: Name, 2: Current Stock, 3: Unit, 4: Min Stock, 5: Supplier
inv_sheet = None
for s in inv_json['sheets']:
    if s['properties']['title'] == 'Material_Inventory':
        inv_sheet = s
        break
if not inv_sheet:
    print(json.dumps({"error":"Material_Inventory sheet not found"}))
    sys.exit(0)

inv_rows = inv_sheet['data'][0]['rowData']

inventory = {}  # material_id -> dict {qty, unit, row}
row_by_material = {}
for idx, row in enumerate(inv_rows[1:], start=2):  # 1-based rows, header is row 1
    vals = row.get('values', [])
    if len(vals) < 4:
        continue
    mid = get_cell_value(vals[0])
    qty = get_cell_value(vals[2])
    unit = get_cell_value(vals[3])
    if not mid:
        continue
    try:
        qty_num = float(qty) if qty is not None else 0.0
    except Exception:
        qty_num = 0.0
    inventory[mid] = {"qty": qty_num, "unit": unit, "row": idx}
    row_by_material[mid] = idx

# Orders list (from tool output). Paste JSON array here.
orders_json = '''[
  {
    "id": 14,
    "status": "processing",
    "date_created": "2025-10-16T22:41:56",
    "date_paid": "2025-10-16T22:41:56",
    "line_items": [
      {"sku": "CHAIR_001", "quantity": 2}
    ]
  },
  {
    "id": 13,
    "status": "processing",
    "date_created": "2025-10-16T22:41:53",
    "date_paid": "2025-10-16T22:41:54",
    "line_items": [
      {"sku": "CHAIR_001", "quantity": 1},
      {"sku": "TABLE_001", "quantity": 4}
    ]
  },
  {
    "id": 12,
    "status": "processing",
    "date_created": "2025-10-16T22:41:51",
    "date_paid": "2025-10-16T22:41:51",
    "line_items": [
      {"sku": "TABLE_001", "quantity": 5},
      {"sku": "DESK_001", "quantity": 2},
      {"sku": "CHAIR_001", "quantity": 5}
    ]
  }
]'''
orders = json.loads(orders_json)

# Compute total ordered quantities per SKU and per order consumptions
sku_totals = defaultdict(int)
for order in orders:
    for li in order.get('line_items', []):
        sku = li.get('sku')
        qty = int(li.get('quantity') or 0)
        if not sku or qty <= 0:
            continue
        sku_totals[sku] += qty

# Compute material consumption
material_consumption = defaultdict(float)
missing_bom_skus = []
for sku, total_qty in sku_totals.items():
    bom_lines = bom_map.get(sku)
    if not bom_lines:
        missing_bom_skus.append(sku)
        continue
    for line in bom_lines:
        material_consumption[line['material_id']] += line['qty_per'] * total_qty

# Apply deduction to inventory
updated_inventory = {}  # material_id -> new_qty
negative_hits = []
missing_inventory_materials = []
for mid, cons in material_consumption.items():
    if mid not in inventory:
        missing_inventory_materials.append(mid)
        continue
    cur = inventory[mid]['qty']
    new_qty = cur - cons
    if new_qty < 0:
        negative_hits.append({"material_id": mid, "consumption": cons, "current": cur, "new": new_qty})
        new_qty = 0.0
    inventory[mid]['qty'] = new_qty
    updated_inventory[mid] = new_qty

# Compute max producible quantities for all finished products in BOM
sku_max_producible = {}
for sku, lines in bom_map.items():
    if not lines:
        sku_max_producible[sku] = 0
        continue
    caps = []
    feasible = True
    for line in lines:
        mid = line['material_id']
        req = line['qty_per']
        if req <= 0:
            continue
        avail = inventory.get(mid, {}).get('qty')
        if avail is None:
            feasible = False
            caps.append(0)
        else:
            caps.append(int(math.floor(avail / req)))
    sku_max_producible[sku] = min(caps) if caps else 0

# Build update plan for sheets: list of {material_id, row, new_qty}
updates_plan = []
for mid, new_qty in updated_inventory.items():
    row = row_by_material.get(mid)
    if row is None:
        continue
    updates_plan.append({"material_id": mid, "row": row, "new_qty": round(new_qty, 6)})

result = {
    "orders_processed": [o['id'] for o in orders],
    "sku_totals": sku_totals,
    "material_consumption": material_consumption,
    "sheet_updates": updates_plan,
    "sku_max_producible": sku_max_producible,
    "missing_bom_skus": missing_bom_skus,
    "missing_inventory_materials": missing_inventory_materials,
    "negative_hits": negative_hits,
}

# Custom JSON serializer for defaultdict
class DF(json.JSONEncoder):
    def default(self, o):
        if isinstance(o, defaultdict):
            return dict(o)
        return json.JSONEncoder.default(self, o)

print(json.dumps(result, cls=DF, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
 code
```

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
import json, math
from pathlib import Path

bom_file = Path('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/a6UVtcwQ5EX9VcjQQeSH2W.json')
inv_file = Path('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/QptEGVUnpG3VPwU6uJytYq.json')

bom_outer = json.loads(bom_file.read_text())
inv_outer = json.loads(inv_file.read_text())

# The actual Sheets JSON is inside the 'text' field as a JSON string
bom_json = json.loads(bom_outer['text'])
inv_json = json.loads(inv_outer['text'])

# Helper to extract cell value

def get_cell_value(cell):
    if not cell:
        return None
    ev = cell.get('effectiveValue') or cell.get('userEnteredValue')
    if not ev:
        return None
    if 'stringValue' in ev:
        return str(ev['stringValue']).strip()
    if 'numberValue' in ev:
        return ev['numberValue']
    if 'boolValue' in ev:
        return ev['boolValue']
    return None

# Parse BOM
bom_sheet = next(s for s in bom_json['sheets'] if s['properties']['title']=='BOM')
rows = bom_sheet['data'][0]['rowData']

from collections import defaultdict
bom_map = defaultdict(list)
for r in rows[1:]:
    vals = r.get('values', [])
    if len(vals) < 5:
        continue
    sku = get_cell_value(vals[0])
    mat = get_cell_value(vals[2])
    qty = get_cell_value(vals[4])
    unit = get_cell_value(vals[5]) if len(vals)>5 else None
    if not sku or not mat or qty is None:
        continue
    try:
        qty = float(qty)
    except:
        continue
    if qty < 0:
        continue
    bom_map[sku].append({'material_id': mat, 'qty_per': qty, 'unit': unit})

# Parse Inventory
inv_sheet = next(s for s in inv_json['sheets'] if s['properties']['title']=='Material_Inventory')
inv_rows = inv_sheet['data'][0]['rowData']

inventory = {}  # material_id -> {qty, unit, row}
row_by_material = {}
for idx, r in enumerate(inv_rows[1:], start=2):
    vals = r.get('values', [])
    if len(vals) < 4:
        continue
    mid = get_cell_value(vals[0])
    qty = get_cell_value(vals[2])
    unit = get_cell_value(vals[3])
    if not mid:
        continue
    try:
        qty = float(qty) if qty is not None else 0.0
    except:
        qty = 0.0
    inventory[mid] = {'qty': qty, 'unit': unit, 'row': idx}
    row_by_material[mid] = idx

# Orders (from last orders_list result)
orders = [
  {
    'id': 14,
    'status': 'processing',
    'line_items': [ {'sku':'CHAIR_001','quantity':2} ]
  },
  {
    'id': 13,
    'status': 'processing',
    'line_items': [ {'sku':'CHAIR_001','quantity':1}, {'sku':'TABLE_001','quantity':4} ]
  },
  {
    'id': 12,
    'status': 'processing',
    'line_items': [ {'sku':'TABLE_001','quantity':5}, {'sku':'DESK_001','quantity':2}, {'sku':'CHAIR_001','quantity':5} ]
  }
]

# Aggregate SKU totals
sku_totals = defaultdict(int)
for o in orders:
    for li in o['line_items']:
        if not li.get('sku'):
            continue
        sku_totals[li['sku']] += int(li.get('quantity') or 0)

# Calculate consumption
material_consumption = defaultdict(float)
missing_bom_skus = []
for sku, qty in sku_totals.items():
    bom_lines = bom_map.get(sku)
    if not bom_lines:
        missing_bom_skus.append(sku)
        continue
    for line in bom_lines:
        material_consumption[line['material_id']] += line['qty_per'] * qty

# Deduct from inventory
updated_materials = {}
negative_hits = []
missing_inventory_materials = []
for mid, cons in material_consumption.items():
    entry = inventory.get(mid)
    if not entry:
        missing_inventory_materials.append(mid)
        continue
    new_qty = entry['qty'] - cons
    if new_qty < 0:
        negative_hits.append({'material_id': mid, 'consumption': cons, 'current': entry['qty'], 'new': new_qty})
        new_qty = 0.0
    entry['qty'] = new_qty
    updated_materials[mid] = {'row': entry['row'], 'new_qty': round(new_qty, 6)}

# Compute max producible quantities per SKU given updated inventory
sku_max = {}
for sku, lines in bom_map.items():
    caps = []
    for line in lines:
        mid = line['material_id']
        req = line['qty_per']
        avail = inventory.get(mid, {}).get('qty')
        if avail is None or req <= 0:
            caps.append(0)
        else:
            caps.append(int(math.floor(avail/req)))
    sku_max[sku] = min(caps) if caps else 0

result = {
    'sku_totals': dict(sku_totals),
    'material_consumption': dict(material_consumption),
    'updated_materials': updated_materials,
    'negative_hits': negative_hits,
    'missing_bom_skus': missing_bom_skus,
    'missing_inventory_materials': missing_inventory_materials,
    'sku_max': sku_max,
}
print(json.dumps(result, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
 code
```


```python
import json
from pathlib import Path
inv_file = Path('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/QptEGVUnpG3VPwU6uJytYq.json')
inv_outer = json.loads(inv_file.read_text())
inv_json = json.loads(inv_outer['text'])
# Material_Inventory sheet
sheet = next(s for s in inv_json['sheets'] if s['properties']['title']=='Material_Inventory')
rows = sheet['data'][0]['rowData']
# Row 10 (1-based) => index 9; Column C (3rd, index 2)
cell = rows[9]['values'][2]
val = None
if 'effectiveValue' in cell and 'numberValue' in cell['effectiveValue']:
    val = cell['effectiveValue']['numberValue']
elif 'userEnteredValue' in cell and 'numberValue' in cell['userEnteredValue']:
    val = cell['userEnteredValue']['numberValue']
print(val) code
```

Operational notes
- I used orders with status processing/completed as “paid” (needs_processing true). If you want this to run continuously on each status change to “processing” or “completed,” you can add a WooCommerce webhook (topic: order.updated) pointing to your automation endpoint. Provide a delivery URL and secret when you’re ready, and I can create it.
- All unit arithmetic assumed the units in BOM align with Material_Inventory (e.g., liters vs. L, m² vs. “square meters”). If you use mixed units for the same material, we should add a conversion map.
